***кинжал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кинжал.html>кинжа́л</a> (5743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nogai_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nogai language">Nogai</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="nog">кынжал</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nog-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kınjal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kumyk_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kumyk language">Kumyk</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kum">хынжал</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kum-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xınjal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crimean_Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Crimean Tatar language">Crimean Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="crh">къанджер</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="crh">ханджер</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="crh">гъанджер</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">хәнҗәр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xäncär</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خنجر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xanjar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинжал.html>кинжа́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kinžál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинжал.html>кинжа́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинжал.html>кинжа́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинжал.html>кинжа́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dagger, poniard (a stabbing weapon)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино</a> (1541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kinó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>movie, motion picture, film
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звуковой.html>звуково́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zvukovóje <b>kinó</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sound film (as opposed to "silent film")</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>movies, cinema, the pictures</li></ol>

***кипеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a> (4476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kypě̀ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kwep-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cupidity</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">covet</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hope</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kipétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закипеть.html>закипе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to boil, to seethe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключо́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kipétʹ ključóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to boil over</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to boil, to rage, to seethe, to burn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of emotions</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́бой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kipétʹ</b> zlóboj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to boil</b> with anger</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be in full swing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of action</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипи́т</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Rabóta <b>kipít</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The work <b>is in full swing</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ки<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>пе́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вскипеть.html>вскипе́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:закипеть.html>закипе́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кип-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипрский.html>ки́прский</a> (31130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Кипр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kipr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипятивший.html>кипяти́вший</a> (16152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипятивший.html>кипяти́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kipjatívšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипятить.html>кипяти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kipjatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***кипятить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипятить.html>кипяти́ть</a> (16152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from the same root as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kipétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to boil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kypě̀ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kwep-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">covet</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hope</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипятить.html>кипяти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kipjatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскипятить.html>вскипяти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
